Predicted Runners — 2025-06-07

Scoring Methodology: Each horse is assigned a model_score, the equal-weighted sum of these standardized features (mean=0, std=1):
  • rpr: Racing Post Rating
  • ofr: Official Rating
  • ts: TopSpeed rating
  • form_points: Points from last 5 finishes (5 for a win, 3 for second, etc.)
  • trainer_14d_pct: Trainer’s win % over past 14 days
  • weight_adj: Weight adjustment [(median weight − this weight) × 0.10]
  • days_since_last: Days since last race (default 30 if none)
  • course_runs: Prior runs at this course
  • dist_runs: Prior runs over this distance
  • going_runs: Prior runs on this going
  • hist_form_score: Inverted avg position over last 6 races
  • jockey_wins_history: Prior wins by this jockey
  • trainer_wins_history: Prior wins by this trainer
Additionally, Comment and Spotlight are shown as the final columns.
